   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading">Crystal Clear</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="vector-body"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikimedia Commons, the free media repository
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" lang="en" dir="ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <p>Original <a href="/wiki/Category:Icons" title="Category:Icons">Icons</a> from the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.everaldo.com/crystal/">Crystal Clear</a><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space: nowrap;">[<em><span title="" class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Link_rot">dead link</a></span></em>]</sup> icon set (<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20121010063705/http://everaldo.com/crystal/">archived page</a> as of 10 October 2012 at Internet Archive) by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Everaldo_Coelho" class="extiw" title="w:Everaldo Coelho">Everaldo Coelho</a>. This set is a previous version of the <a href="/wiki/Category:Crystal_Project" title="Category:Crystal Project">Crystal Project</a> icon set. </p>
      <p>The icons are <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.everaldo.com/crystal/?action=license">licensed</a><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space: nowrap;">[<em><span title="" class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Link_rot">dead link</a></span></em>]</sup> under the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GNU_Lesser_General_Public_License" class="extiw" title="w:GNU Lesser General Public License">GNU Lesser General Public License</a> (LGPL). </p>
      <p>These icons can be downloaded in a single package at <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://sourceforge.net/projects/openiconlibrary/">Open Icon Library</a>. </p>
      <p>You can also view these icons <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Clear_by_type" title="Crystal Clear by type">sorted by type</a>. </p>
      <p>All images’ real size is <b>128px</b> in PNG format. For reproduced or derivative SVG work, see <a href="/wiki/Category:SVG_Crystal_Clear_icons" title="Category:SVG Crystal Clear icons">Category:SVG Crystal Clear icons</a>. </p>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Devices">Devices</span></h2>
